Aggregated timing (signed slack from timing engine; score uses +violation):
  WNS_SS = min_p slack_ss[p]
  TNS_SS = sum_{p: slack_ss[p]<0} slack_ss[p]
  WNS_FF = min_p slack_ff[p]
  TNS_FF = sum_{p: slack_ff[p]<0} slack_ff[p]

Area model (PG evaluation):
  Area = sum_{e: EXISTING_BUF} area_wt[e]
       + sum_{e: INSERTABLE, d_ss[e]>0} area_wt[e]

Maximize Score (alpha=beta=gamma=1); WNS/TNS terms use positive violations:
  WNS_SS+ = max(0, -WNS_SS)   TNS_SS+ = max(0, -TNS_SS)
  WNS_FF+ = max(0, -WNS_FF)   TNS_FF+ = max(0, -TNS_FF)
  Score = (1 - TNS_SS+/TNS_SS+_ori) + (1 - WNS_SS+/WNS_SS+_ori)
        + (1 - TNS_FF+/TNS_FF+_ori) + (1 - WNS_FF+/WNS_FF+_ori)
        + (1 - Area/Area_ori)

PG minimizes obj = -Score via projected subgradient on d_ss, d_ff with
box constraints above (project_bounds after each step).
